Swordsman Dojo

Crystal Cave

- You **cannot leave** the realm with **Realm Units **you obtain within the realm, with one exception..

- You keep any **Items** you obtain in the realm

- In the realm you can summon from one of **3 TRIALS** (Banners)
- **11x New Realm Units** obtainable only in the realm

- Each **Banner **is summoned with one of **3 Currencies** (Aqua, Solar and Flame Tokens)
- **Aqua**, **Solar** and **Flame Tokens** are obtained based on the maps and challenges you play
- You must **choose **what path you want to grind for that will give you the token you want to summon with
- There will be secret pity on these banners

**NEW ATHENYX BATTLEPASS**
- In the realm you will get a **F2P** + **Premium** Battlepass
- It will have **25 Tiers**
- It will be **Resettable** when you reach the end of the battlepass so you can play it again
- The goal of the battlepass is to grind for **Athenyx's Key** and **Athenyx's Tether** (to exit the realm + take a unit back)
